GT Equivalence Verification (CRK34)
============================================================
GT: -c0*A**c1 + c2*_f*A**c3
Candidate formulas: 69

GT is the fixed function (independent of \(t\)):
\[
0.7240016388253205\,A^{1/3}\;-\;0.1689114325901851\,A^2.
\]
So any matching candidate must (i) have no unavoidable \(t\)-dependence, and (ii) be expressible exactly as a linear combination of \(A^{1/3}\) and \(A^2\) with those coefficients, with no extra constant term, no \(A\) term, no \(\lvert A\rvert\) unless it can be removed, etc.

---

### 1. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + A^{c2}c3\sin(c4 t+c5)+c6 t^{c7}+c8\)
To remove \(t\): set \(c3=0\) and \(c6=0\). Then expression is \(A^2c0+Ac1+c8\). GT has no \(A\) or constant term, so need \(c1=0,c8=0\). Then only \(A^2\) remains; cannot produce \(A^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 2. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^2c1 + A^{c2}c3\sin(Ac4+c5)\cos(c6 t)+c7\)
Remove \(t\): set \(c3=0\) (or \(c6=0\) still leaves \(\cos(0)=1\) but \(\sin(Ac4+c5)\) remains). Best: \(c3=0\). Then \(A^{1/3}c0+A^2c1+c7\). Set \(c7=0\). Choose \(c0=0.7240016388253205\), \(c1=-0.1689114325901851\). **Yes, matches.**

### 3. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^2c1 + c2 + c3\sin(c4\log(c5|A|+c6 t^2+1)+c7)\)
To remove \(t\): must set \(c3=0\) (since \(t^2\) is inside log). Then \(A^{1/3}c0+A^2c1+c2\). Set \(c2=0\) and pick \(c0,c1\) as GT. **Yes.**

### 4. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^2c1\)
Directly matches by setting \(c0=0.7240016388253205\), \(c1=-0.1689114325901851\). **Yes.**

### 5. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^2c1 + c2\)
Set \(c2=0\), then same as (4). **Yes.**

### 6. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^2c1 + A^2c2 + c3\)
Combine \(A^2\) terms: \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^2(c1+c2)+c3\). Set \(c3=0\), choose \(c0\) as GT and \(c1+c2=-0.1689...\). **Yes.**

### 7. \(A^2c0 + c1 + c2|A|^{1/3}\)
Has \(|A|^{1/3}\), not \(A^{1/3}\). Unless domain restricted to \(A\ge 0\) (not allowed here), cannot equal for all real \(A\). If set \(c2=0\), lose \(A^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 8. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^2c1 + A^2c2 + Ac3 + c4\)
Need no \(A\) or constant: set \(c3=0,c4=0\). Then \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^2(c1+c2)\). Choose coefficients to match GT. **Yes.**

### 9. \(A^{c0}c1 + c2 + c3|A+c4|^{c5}\)
To get exactly two power terms \(A^{1/3}\) and \(A^2\) without absolute/shift: would need \(c4=0\) and avoid absolute (still \(|A|^{c5}\)). That cannot equal \(A^{1/3}\) for negative \(A\). If kill that term, you only have one power. **No.**

### 10. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + c2 + c3|A|^{c4}\)
Same issue: \(|A|^{c4}\) cannot equal \(A^{1/3}\) for all real \(A\). If set \(c3=0\), cannot get \(A^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 11. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + A^{c2}c3 + c4\)
Can match: set \(c1=0,c4=0\). Choose \(c0=-0.1689114325901851\). For the other term set \(c2=1/3\), \(c3=0.7240016388253205\). Then \(A^2c0 + A^{1/3}c3\) equals GT. **Yes.**

### 12. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^2c1 + Ac2 + c3\)
Set \(c2=0,c3=0\), choose \(c0,c1\) as GT. **Yes.**

### 13. \(A^{1/3}c0 + c1 + c2|A+c3|^2\)
\(|A+c3|^2=(A+c3)^2\) but includes shift unless \(c3=0\). With \(c3=0\), term is \(c2A^2\) (since \(|A|^2=A^2\)). Then expression \(A^{1/3}c0 + c2A^2 + c1\). Set \(c1=0\), choose \(c0\) and \(c2=-0.1689...\). **Yes.**

### 14. \(A^{c0}c1 + A^{c2}c3 + c4\)
Set \(c4=0\). Choose \((c0,c1)=(1/3,0.7240016388253205)\) and \((c2,c3)=(2,-0.1689114325901851)\). **Yes.**

### 15. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^2c1 + c2 + c3\log(c4|A|^{c5}+1)\)
To match GT exactly, must remove log term: set \(c3=0\). Then set \(c2=0\) and choose \(c0,c1\) as GT. **Yes.**

### 16. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^2c1 + A^{c2}c3 + c4\)
Set \(c3=0,c4=0\) and match via \(c0,c1\). **Yes.**

### 17. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^2c1 + c2 + c3\log(c4\exp(A^{1/3}c5 + c6\sin(c7 t+c8))+1)\)
Contains unavoidable \(t\) inside log unless \(c3=0\). Set \(c3=0\), then reduce to \(A^{1/3}c0+A^2c1+c2\). Set \(c2=0\), choose \(c0,c1\) as GT. **Yes.**

### 18. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^2c1 + c2 + c3\log(Ac4+1)\)
Set \(c3=0\), \(c2=0\), choose \(c0,c1\) as GT. **Yes.**

### 19. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^2c1 + \frac{Ac2}{Ac3+c4} + c5 + \frac{c6}{Ac3+c4}\)
To eliminate rational dependence on \(A\): set \(c2=0,c6=0\). Then \(A^{1/3}c0+A^2c1+c5\). Set \(c5=0\), choose \(c0,c1\) as GT. **Yes.**

### 20. \(A^{c0}c1 + A^{c2}c3\exp(c4|A|) + c5\)
The \(\exp(c4|A|)\) cannot be made a pure power term unless \(c4=0\), giving \(A^{c2}c3\). Then we have two power terms plus constant: set \(c5=0\), choose exponents \(c0=1/3,c2=2\) and coefficients \(c1=0.7240...,c3=-0.1689...\). **Yes.**

### 21. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^2c1 + c2\exp(c3 t) + c4\)
Remove \(t\): set \(c2=0\). Then \(A^{1/3}c0+A^2c1+c4\). Set \(c4=0\), choose \(c0,c1\) as GT. **Yes.**

### 22. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^2c1 + Ac2\exp(c3 t) + c4\)
Remove \(t\): must set \(c2=0\). Then same as (21): set \(c4=0\), choose \(c0,c1\). **Yes.**

### 23. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^2c1 + c2 + c3\exp(c4 t)\log(Ac5+1)\)
To remove \(t\): set \(c3=0\). Then \(A^{1/3}c0+A^2c1+c2\). Set \(c2=0\), choose \(c0,c1\). **Yes.**

### 24. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^2c1 + c2 + c3\log(c4\exp(Ac5+c6 t)+1)\)
Has \(t\) inside log unless \(c3=0\) (or \(c6=0\) still leaves log(exp(Ac5)) non-polynomial). Set \(c3=0\). Then match as usual with \(c2=0\). **Yes.**

### 25. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^2c1 + c2 + c3\exp(c4 t)|A|^{c5}\)
To remove \(t\): set \(c3=0\). Then match with \(c2=0\). **Yes.**

### 26. \(A\cdot A^{c0}c1 + A^{c0}c2 + A^{c3}c4 + c5\)
This is \(c1 A^{c0+1} + c2 A^{c0} + c4 A^{c3} + c5\). Can choose to keep exactly two terms: set \(c5=0\), set one coefficient to 0. For instance set \(c1=0\), choose \(c0=1/3,c2=0.7240...\); choose \(c3=2,c4=-0.1689...\). **Yes.**

### 27. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^2c1 + Ac2(c3+t)^{c4} + c5\)
Remove \(t\): set \(c2=0\). Then \(A^{1/3}c0+A^2c1+c5\). Set \(c5=0\), choose \(c0,c1\). **Yes.**

### 28. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^2c1 + Ac2(c3+|t|)^{c4} + c5\)
Same: set \(c2=0\), \(c5=0\), choose \(c0,c1\). **Yes.**

### 29. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^2c1 + \frac{Ac2}{c3 t+c4} + c5 + \frac{c6}{c3 t+c4}\)
To remove \(t\): must set \(c2=0,c6=0\). Then \(A^{1/3}c0+A^2c1+c5\). Set \(c5=0\), choose \(c0,c1\). **Yes.**

### 30. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^2c1 + Ac2\exp(Ac3) + c4\)
To match GT, must remove extra non-power term: set \(c2=0\). Then set \(c4=0\), choose \(c0,c1\). **Yes.**

### 31. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^2c1 + c2\exp(Ac3) + c4\)
Set \(c2=0\), \(c4=0\), choose \(c0,c1\). **Yes.**

### 32. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^2c1 + c2\sin(Ac3+c4) + c5\)
Set \(c2=0\), \(c5=0\), choose \(c0,c1\). **Yes.**

### 33. \(A^{c0}c1 + A^{c2}c3(c4 t+1)^{c5} + c6\)
Remove \(t\): set \(c3=0\) (or \(c5=0\) makes \((c4 t+1)^0=1\) leaving a pure power term; either works). Then with \(c3=0\), expression \(A^{c0}c1+c6\) cannot make two terms. If instead keep second term and remove \(t\) via \(c5=0\): then second term becomes \(A^{c2}c3\). Set \(c6=0\). Choose \(c0=1/3,c1=0.7240...\) and \(c2=2,c3=-0.1689...\). **Yes.**

### 34. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + A^{c2}c3\exp(c4 t) + c5\)
Remove \(t\): set \(c3=0\). Then \(A^2c0+Ac1+c5\). Cannot produce \(A^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 35. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^2c1 + c2 + \frac{c3 t}{Ac4+c5} + \frac{c6}{Ac4+c5}\)
Remove \(t\): set \(c3=0\). Remaining rational term \(\frac{c6}{Ac4+c5}\) must be removed: set \(c6=0\). Then match with \(c2=0\), choose \(c0,c1\). **Yes.**

### 36. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^2c1 + c2 + \frac{c3 t}{c4 t+c5} + \frac{c6}{c4 t+c5}\)
To remove \(t\): easiest set \(c3=0,c6=0\). Then match with \(c2=0\), choose \(c0,c1\). **Yes.**

### 37. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + c2|A|^{c3} + c4 t^{c5} + c6\)
Remove \(t\): set \(c4=0\). Need \(A^{1/3}\) but term is \(|A|^{c3}\) which can’t equal \(A^{1/3}\) for all real \(A\). If set \(c2=0\), lose it. **No.**

### 38. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + A^{c2}c3 + c4 t^{c5} + c6\)
Remove \(t\): set \(c4=0\). Remove \(A\) and constant: set \(c1=0,c6=0\). Then choose \(c0=-0.1689...\), \(c2=1/3\), \(c3=0.7240...\). **Yes.**

### 39. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^2c1 + Ac2\max(0,c3+t)^{c4} + c5\)

Even if set \(c2=0\), the \(|A|^{c6}\) cannot equal \(A^{1/3}\) for all real \(A\). If set \(c5=0\), then only polynomial/constant terms remain, no \(A^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 47. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + A^{c2}c3 + c4\exp(Ac5) + c6\)

### 49. \(A^{1/3}c0\exp(Ac1) + A^2c2 + Ac3 + c4\exp(Ac5) + c6\)

### 51. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + \frac{c2}{c3+t} + c4\log(A^{c5}c6+c7)\)

### 62. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^2c1 + c2 + c3\log(Ac4 + c5\sin(c6e^{c7 t}+c8)+1)\)

### 63. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + A^{c2}c3e^{Ac4} + c5e^{Ac6} + c7\)

### 64. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + \frac{Ac2}{(Ac3+1)^2} + c4e^{Ac5} + c6\)

### 65. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + A^{c2}c3\sin(Ac4+c5)\cos(c6 t) + c7\)

### 66. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + c2 + c3\sin(Ac4+c5)/\sqrt{A}\)
The last term is \(\sin(\cdot)A^{-1/2}\), not a pure \(A^{1/3}\) term; cannot equal \(A^{1/3}\) for all \(A\). If set \(c3=0\), no \(A^{1/3}\). **No.**

### 67. \(c0 + c1\log(A^{1/3}c2+c3) + c4\sin(Ac5+c6)\)

### 68. \(c0 + c1\log(A^{c2}c3+c4) + c5\sin(Ac6+c7)\)
Same: to remove non-algebraic terms set \(c1=0,c5=0\) leaving constant only. **No.**

Log term cannot equal \(A^{1/3}\) for all \(A\); if set \(c2=0\), no \(A^{1/3}\). **No.**
